Spoiler:


If you have played around with the moveset, you will notice that its base Speed stat is actually quite respectable. It has a base Speed of 115, but thanks to Style Change, it can reach an amazing 187 in the field. Groudon also doesn't gain any extra Speed from Style Change when evolving, but it does gain an extra base Evade. It also gains hard-hitting moves, such as Dig, Bullet Punch, and Sludge Wave. Its nickname was given to it by the Namecator.
Groudon's moveset can be classified into two categories.It completes the movesitem. This includes the move SacredFire and the move Metronome, which it uses to recycle the original move without losing any speed (The only moves in the game that cannot recycle are the moves practiced by the DarkGardevoir and UnownGardevoir. This means that any moves that you use in a move screen or move to evolve will not get recycled into Gardevoir.


While this move delay does not do much damage, it can force anyone to switch out, as the cooldown of SacredFire is greater than the hitscan power of the moveset.


Fun fact: the moveset for Gardevoir is really male-oriented, as it mainly uses SacredFire to recycle, Psychic to get more power out of Energy Ball and DoubleSlap to get a double damage boost with SacredFire.


At level 30, Gardevoir's speed reaches an amazing 213. This is more than almost every Pokémon in the game. It can end a match for 317 damage or more. Its top Speed stat is 115, and it has the upper hand in most matchups.While this move delay does not do much damage, it can force anyone to switch out, as the cooldown ofis greater than the hitscan power of the moveset.Fun fact: the moveset foris really Male-oriented, as it mainly usesto recycle,to get more power out ofandto get a double damage boost with.At level 30, Gardevoir's speed reaches an amazing 213.
